Compiled from various sources including Marshall County Tennessee Cemeteries & updated with permission by a few of the findagrave.com listings. Other grave listings were contributed
by others. 99% of the compilation effort was by Faye Bradford during the months of August & September of 2011. Added here 18 Sep 2011 by Wayne Austin. Some of these listings
were presented by the book Cemeteries of Marshall County by Tim & Helen Marsh and previous to that in the 1960s in a book by Ralph Whitesell. Revised again by the efforts of Mary
Bob McClain with organization by Faye Bradford 12 Nov 2012
